#### [@yardinternet/gutenberg-cards@1.0.16](https://github.com/yardinternet/gutenberg-packages/compare/@yardinternet/gutenberg-cards@1.0.15...@yardinternet/gutenberg-cards@1.0.16)

- (chore): move dev-deps to root package.json [`9675bfb`](https://github.com/yardinternet/gutenberg-packages/commit/9675bfb04ab5e6877e0ff121cae17e2822ac9008)
